s-225.272,467,-225.272,467s-235,486,-235,486c-2.7,4.7,-9,7,-19,7
c-6,0,-10,-1,-12,-3s-194,-422,-194,-422s-65,47,-65,47z
M834 80h400000v40h-400000z"></path></svg></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1133em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span> — typically cuts activation memory by 5–10×.</p>
<h2 id="the-lora-cheat">The LoRA cheat<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#the-lora-cheat">#</a></h2>
<p>LoRA changes the picture dramatically because <strong>only the adapter params get gradients + optimizer states</strong>. Let <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span></span></span></span> = base params, <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord text mtight"><span class="mord mtight">LoRA</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> = LoRA params (typically 0.1–1% of <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span></span></span></span>).</p>
<pre><code>LoRA training ≈ 2P (frozen weights)        ← bf16, no grads
              + 16 × P_LoRA                ← grads + Adam on tiny matrices
              + activations                ← still depend on full forward!
</code></pre>
<p>Concrete: 7B in bf16, LoRA with r=16 on all linears, ~40M trainable params:</p>
<ul>
<li>Frozen weights: 14 GB</li>
<li>LoRA grads + optimizer: <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7278em;vertical-align:-0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">16</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">40</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">M</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0.6</span></span></span></span> GB</li>
<li>Activations: maybe 5–15 GB depending on batch/seq</li>
</ul>
<p>Total ~20–30 GB. Fits an A6000 or even a 3090 with checkpointing.</p>
<h2 id="qlora-the-further-cheat">QLoRA — the further cheat<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#qlora-the-further-cheat">#</a></h2>
<p>Quantize the frozen base to 4-bit NF4:</p>
<ul>
<li>Frozen weights: <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7667em;vertical-align:-0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">7</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">B</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0.5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">3.5</span></span></span></span> GB (was 14)</li>
<li>LoRA grads + optimizer: ~0.6 GB</li>
<li>Activations: same</li>
</ul>
<p>Total ~10–15 GB. <strong>This is why a 65B model fits on one A100-80GB</strong> — it goes from ~130 GB frozen to ~32.5 GB frozen.</p>
<h2 id="quick-estimation-workflow">Quick estimation workflow<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#quick-estimation-workflow">#</a></h2>
<p>When someone asks "will this fit?":</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Weights</strong>: params × bytes (2 for bf16, 0.5 for 4-bit).</li>
<li><strong>Mode</strong>:
<ul>
<li>Inference → add KV cache (≈ 0.5 MB/token for 7B-class, scales with model size).</li>
<li>Full FT → multiply weights cost by ~8 (so bf16 weights × 8 ≈ training static cost).</li>
<li>LoRA → just weights cost + ~1 GB for adapters.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Activations</strong>: rough guess <code>batch × seq × 0.5 MB</code> for 7B-class without checkpointing; divide by ~5 with checkpointing.</li>
<li>Add 10–20% slop for fragmentation, CUDA workspace, etc.</li>
</ol>
<h2 id="sanity-check-examples">Sanity check examples<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#sanity-check-examples">#</a></h2>

































<table><thead><tr><th>Setup</th><th>Memory</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>7B inference, bf16, seq=2k, bs=1</td><td>~16 GB</td></tr><tr><td>7B inference, bf16, seq=32k, bs=1</td><td>~30 GB (KV dominates)</td></tr><tr><td>7B full FT, bf16, bs=4, seq=2k</td><td>~110 GB + activations → multi-GPU</td></tr><tr><td>7B LoRA, bf16, bs=4, seq=2k</td><td>~25 GB → single 3090/A6000</td></tr><tr><td>7B QLoRA, bs=4, seq=2k</td><td>~12 GB → single 4090</td></tr><tr><td>70B QLoRA, bs=1, seq=2k</td><td>~45 GB → single A100-80GB</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The mental shortcut I actually use: <strong>bf16 inference ≈ 2× params in GB. Full FT ≈ 16× params in GB. LoRA training ≈ inference cost + a bit. QLoRA ≈ inference cost / 4.</strong></p>
<h3 id="practical-indications">Practical Indications<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#practical-indications">#</a></h3>
<h4 id="when-lora-is-feasible">When LoRA is Feasible<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#when-lora-is-feasible">#</a></h4>
<p>Low-rank updates tend to be sufficient when:</p>
<ul>
<li>the pretrained model already contains the necessary capabilities;</li>
<li>fine-tuning primarily needs to select, redirect, or reweight those capabilities;</li>
<li>the new task is close to pretraining;</li>
<li>the dataset is relatively small.</li>
</ul>
<p>They are less reliable when adaptation requires:</p>
<ul>
<li>learning a large amount of new domain knowledge;</li>
<li>continued pretraining on billions of tokens;</li>
<li>major changes to representations;</li>
<li>difficult mathematics, code or reasoning specialization;</li>
<li>adapting a weak base model to a substantially different target distribution.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="comparing-to-rag">Comparing to RAG<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#comparing-to-rag">#</a></h4>









































<table><thead><tr><th>Requirement</th><th>Better default</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Teach response style or behaviour</td><td>LoRA</td></tr><tr><td>Teach domain terminology and recurring patterns</td><td>LoRA</td></tr><tr><td>Store a moderate, stable body of knowledge</td><td>LoRA may work</td></tr><tr><td>Store thousands of changing facts</td><td>RAG</td></tr><tr><td>Require citations or source traceability</td><td>RAG</td></tr><tr><td>Correct or delete one fact quickly</td><td>RAG or model editing</td></tr><tr><td>Work without retrieval infrastructure</td><td>LoRA</td></tr><tr><td>Combine internalised behaviour with current facts</td><td>LoRA + RAG</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2 id="lora-as-parametric-knowledge-memory">LoRA as Parametric Knowledge Memory<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#lora-as-parametric-knowledge-memory">#</a></h2>
<h3 id="what-it-means-for-information-to-be-inside-a-lora">What It Means for Information to Be “Inside” a LoRA<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#what-it-means-for-information-to-be-inside-a-lora">#</a></h3>
<h4 id="knowledge-is-stored-in-the-adapterbackbone-interaction">Knowledge Is Stored in the Adapter–Backbone Interaction<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#knowledge-is-stored-in-the-adapterbackbone-interaction">#</a></h4>
<p>For an adapted model,</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.0361em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1076em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1076em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3173em;"><span style="top:-2.357em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.143em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">ϕ</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:2em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">ϕ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">ℓ</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0502em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">ℓ</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose"><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">ℓ</span><span class="mrel mtight">∈</span><span class="mord mathcal mtight" style="margin-right:0.075em;">S</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1774em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>the base parameters <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">Θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> remain frozen, while <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">ϕ</span></span></span></span> denotes the LoRA parameters attached to the selected modules <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.075em;">S</span></span></span></span>.</p>
<div class="callout" data-callout="note">
<div class="callout-title"><span class="callout-icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M12 20h9"></path><path d="M16.5 3.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L7 19l-4 1 1-4Z"></path></svg></span><span class="callout-title-inner">The Central Ontological Point</span></div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>A LoRA adapter is generally <strong>not a self-contained database</strong>. It stores a parameterized intervention that changes how a particular frozen model processes and retrieves information.</p></div>
</div>
<p>The learned knowledge is therefore distributed across:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Base representations</strong>: entities, syntax, semantic features, reasoning primitives.</li>
<li><strong>Adapter parameters</strong>: task-specific redirection, association, suppression, or recombination.</li>
<li><strong>Prompt</strong>: the key used to activate the relevant modified computation.</li>
<li><strong>Decoder dynamics</strong>: the autoregressive process that reconstructs the answer.</li>
</ul>
<p>Consequences:</p>
<ul>
<li>The same adapter attached to a different base-model revision may fail.</li>
<li>Removing the adapter usually removes the newly acquired behaviour.</li>
<li>Merging <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span></span> into <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">W</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> does not change the represented function; it only changes deployment form.</li>
<li>A small adapter can exploit a large amount of pre-existing structure in the base model.</li>
<li>Adapter size alone does not measure the total complexity of the resulting model.</li>
</ul>
<p>A better conceptual expression is:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">learned response</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">base knowledge</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">adapter intervention</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">prompt-conditioned retrieval</span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<h4 id="residual-information-rather-than-total-information">Residual Information Rather Than Total Information<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#residual-information-rather-than-total-information">#</a></h4>
<p>The adapter need not encode an entire fact from scratch. It must encode only the information that is not already predictable from the frozen model.</p>
<p>Let <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">Z</span></span></span></span> denote the target fact and <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">Θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> the frozen model. The relevant information burden is closer to:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0813em;">H</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">Z</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∣</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">Θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>rather than the unconditional entropy <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0813em;">H</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">Z</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>Examples:</p>

































<table><thead><tr><th align="left">New information</th><th align="left">Residual burden on the adapter</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td align="left">“Paris is a city”</td><td align="left">Almost none; already strongly represented</td></tr><tr><td align="left">“Project Helios uses protocol XJ-17”</td><td align="left">Entity–attribute association may be genuinely new</td></tr><tr><td align="left">A random 10-digit number assigned to a fictional name</td><td align="left">High-entropy arbitrary association</td></tr><tr><td align="left">A new response style</td><td align="left">Low-dimensional behavioural change</td></tr><tr><td align="left">A new mathematical technique</td><td align="left">Potentially requires knowledge, representations, and procedures</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Reversing a well-established fact</td><td align="left">Must overcome an opposing prior in the base model</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="callout" data-callout="note">
<div class="callout-title"><span class="callout-icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M12 20h9"></path><path d="M16.5 3.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L7 19l-4 1 1-4Z"></path></svg></span><span class="callout-title-inner">Conditional Capacity</span></div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>The same number of LoRA parameters can appear to store very different quantities of knowledge because the frozen backbone supplies different amounts of reusable structure.</p></div>
</div>
<p>This is analogous to Conditional Kolmogorov Complexity: the relevant question is not “How long is the fact?” but “How difficult is the fact to specify given what the model already knows?”</p>
<h4 id="memorization-internalization-and-capability-acquisition">Memorization, Internalization, and Capability Acquisition<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#memorization-internalization-and-capability-acquisition">#</a></h4>
<p>These terms should not be treated as synonyms.</p>













































<table><thead><tr><th align="left">Process</th><th align="left">Operational meaning</th><th align="left">Typical evaluation</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td align="left"><strong>Verbatim memorization</strong></td><td align="left">Reproduce an exact target sequence</td><td align="left">Exact match</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Associative memory</strong></td><td align="left">Recover a value from a learned key</td><td align="left">Key–value recall</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Factual internalization</strong></td><td align="left">Answer semantically equivalent questions about a fact</td><td align="left">Paraphrase QA</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Knowledge revision</strong></td><td align="left">Replace or qualify an existing model belief</td><td align="left">Counterfactual editing</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Relational generalization</strong></td><td align="left">Apply learned relations to unseen combinations</td><td align="left">Held-out compositions</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Capability acquisition</strong></td><td align="left">Learn a reusable procedure or algorithm</td><td align="left">Out-of-distribution task performance</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Behavioural adaptation</strong></td><td align="left">Modify style, policy, format, or preference</td><td align="left">Behavioural benchmark</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>A LoRA may achieve high training-set exact match while failing factual internalization. Conversely, it may learn a useful behaviour without storing many discrete facts.</p>
<div class="callout" data-callout="warning">
<div class="callout-title"><span class="callout-icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="m21.73 18-8-14a2 2 0 0 0-3.48 0l-8 14A2 2 0 0 0 4 21h16a2 2 0 0 0 1.73-3Z"></path><path d="M12 9v4"></path><path d="M12 17h.01"></path></svg></span><span class="callout-title-inner">Category Error</span></div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>“The adapter reproduced 10,000 answers” does not imply that it learned 10,000 robust, independently addressable facts.</p></div>
</div>
<h2 id="parameter-count-rank-and-functional-capacity">Parameter Count, Rank, and Functional Capacity<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#parameter-count-rank-and-functional-capacity">#</a></h2>
<h3 id="counting-lora-parameters-correctly">Counting LoRA Parameters Correctly<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#counting-lora-parameters-correctly">#</a></h3>
<h4 id="raw-trainable-parameters">Raw Trainable Parameters<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#raw-trainable-parameters">#</a></h4>
<p>For one matrix <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7224em;vertical-align:-0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">W</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7713em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.7713em;"><span style="top:-3.063em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span><span class="mbin mtight">×</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>,</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">W</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8778em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:2em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.0158em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8213em;"><span style="top:-3.113em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span><span class="mbin mtight">×</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:2em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8213em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8213em;"><span style="top:-3.113em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mbin mtight">×</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>The raw trainable parameter count is:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0139em;">raw</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Across a set of adapted modules <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.075em;">S</span></span></span></span>:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">LoRA</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:2.3795em;vertical-align:-1.3295em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.05em;"><span style="top:-1.8479em;margin-left:0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">ℓ</span><span class="mrel mtight">∈</span><span class="mord mathcal mtight" style="margin-right:0.075em;">S</span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.3295em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0278em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">ℓ</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">in</span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mtight">ℓ</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">out</span></span><span class="mpunct mtight">,</span><span class="mord mtight">ℓ</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;">)</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Under fixed module placement and uniform rank:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">LoRA</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∝</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Doubling <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span> therefore doubles the number of stored scalar parameters, but it does <strong>not</strong> imply doubling useful memory.</p>
<h4 id="independent-degrees-of-freedom">Independent Degrees of Freedom<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#independent-degrees-of-freedom">#</a></h4>
<p>The factorization <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span></span> is non-identifiable because, for any invertible matrix <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7224em;vertical-align:-0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7713em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbb">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.7713em;"><span style="top:-3.063em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mbin mtight">×</span><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>,</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.1141em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8641em;"><span style="top:-3.113em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">−</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Multiple <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span> pairs therefore represent the same update matrix.</p>
<p>The manifold of rank-<span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span> matrices has dimension:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">DoF</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6667em;vertical-align:-0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>The difference is:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0139em;">raw</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">DoF</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8641em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8641em;"><span style="top:-3.113em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Interpretation:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span> counts stored trainable scalars.</li>
<li><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6667em;vertical-align:-0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span> counts the effective local degrees of freedom of the resulting matrix.</li>
<li><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8141em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8141em;"><span style="top:-3.063em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> degrees correspond to redundant changes of basis within the latent rank-<span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span> space.</li>
<li>At small <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span>, this distinction is minor.</li>
<li>At large <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span>, raw parameter count increasingly overstates functional freedom.</li>
</ul>
<div class="callout" data-callout="note">
<div class="callout-title"><span class="callout-icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M12 20h9"></path><path d="M16.5 3.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L7 19l-4 1 1-4Z"></path></svg></span><span class="callout-title-inner">Rank Is a Geometric Constraint</span></div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>Rank does not merely reduce the number of parameters. It constrains every column and row update to pass through a shared <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span>-dimensional latent channel.</p></div>
</div>
<h4 id="scaling-alpha-does-not-add-capacity">Scaling <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span> Does Not Add Capacity<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#scaling-alpha-does-not-add-capacity">#</a></h4>
<p>For:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">W</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.7936em;vertical-align:-0.686em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.1076em;"><span style="top:-2.314em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width:0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top:-3.677em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.686em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span>
<p><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span> changes the scale of the accessible update but not the rank of <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">W</span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>Therefore:</p>
<ul>
<li>Increasing <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span> can improve optimization when updates are too weak.</li>
<li>Excessive <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span> can destabilize training or overwrite base behaviour.</li>
<li>Increasing <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span> does not create new independent directions.</li>
<li>A rank-<span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">8</span></span></span></span> adapter with large <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span> remains rank at most <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">8</span></span></span></span>.</li>
</ul>
<p>This distinguishes:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Capacity limitation</strong>: insufficient update directions.</li>
<li><strong>Optimization limitation</strong>: available directions exist but are not learned effectively.</li>
<li><strong>Scaling limitation</strong>: update directions are learned but have insufficient or excessive magnitude.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="worked-all-linear-parameter-estimate">Worked All-Linear Parameter Estimate<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#worked-all-linear-parameter-estimate">#</a></h4>
<p>Consider a hypothetical 32-layer transformer with:</p>
<ul>
<li>model width <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">4096</span></span></span></span>;</li>
<li>MLP width <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8444em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0778em;">ff</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">14336</span></span></span></span>;</li>
<li>query and output widths <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">4096</span></span></span></span>;</li>
<li>grouped-query key/value widths <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1024</span></span></span></span>;</li>
<li>LoRA applied to <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8778em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">K</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.2222em;">V</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">O</span></span></span></span>, gate, up, and down projections.</li>
</ul>
<p>Parameters per layer are:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:4.2em;vertical-align:-1.85em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mtable"><span class="col-align-r"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:2.35em;"><span style="top:-4.51em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">attn</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3.01em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span><span style="top:-1.51em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.85em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="col-align-l"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:2.35em;"><span class="mord">4096</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord">4096</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">4096</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord">1024</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.01em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">4096</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord">1024</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">4096</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span
