class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0778em;">eff</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:3em;vertical-align:-1.25em;"></span><span class="mop">min</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;"><span class="delimsizing size4">{</span></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.6787em;"><span style="top:-2.3057em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="position:relative;top:0em;">∑</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8043em;"><span style="top:-2.4003em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3.2029em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2997em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">σ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.7959em;"><span style="top:-2.4231em;margin-left:-0.0359em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.0448em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2769em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3.23em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width:0.04em;"></span></span><span style="top:-3.6897em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mop"><span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="position:relative;top:0em;">∑</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.989em;"><span style="top:-2.4003em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3.2029em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2997em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0359em;">σ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.8141em;"><span style="top:-2.4413em;margin-left:-0.0359em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span><span style="top:-3.063em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2587em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.994em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">ρ</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;"><span class="delimsizing size4">}</span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>If <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">128</span></span></span></span> but <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0278em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0778em;">eff</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">0.95</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">12</span></span></span></span>, most nominal directions contribute little update energy.</p>
<p>Possible causes:</p>
<ul>
<li>data do not require the additional directions;</li>
<li>optimization fails to activate them;</li>
<li>regularization suppresses them;</li>
<li>module placement is inappropriate;</li>
<li>the task itself has low intrinsic dimension.</li>
</ul>
<div class="callout" data-callout="note">
<div class="callout-title"><span class="callout-icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M12 20h9"></path><path d="M16.5 3.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L7 19l-4 1 1-4Z"></path></svg></span><span class="callout-title-inner">Diagnostic Rule</span></div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>When performance saturates as nominal rank rises, inspect the singular spectrum before concluding that the task is intrinsically low-rank.</p></div>
</div>
<h4 id="training-data-format">Training Data Format<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#training-data-format">#</a></h4>
<p>Back et al. find that, for knowledge internalization, structured synthetic supervision outperforms raw-text training. Their observed ordering was approximately:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8778em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">QA</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8778em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Summary</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7224em;vertical-align:-0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Rewrite</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Raw text</span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>QA also produced the largest gain per training token, although part of this benefit may arise from alignment between the training and evaluation formats. [S4]</p>
<p>The implication is that capacity depends on <strong>supervision density</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Raw text contains many tokens unrelated to the fact that must be retrieved.</li>
<li>Summaries compress high-value content.</li>
<li>QA pairs expose an explicit key–value relationship.</li>
<li>Multiple paraphrases teach prompt invariance.</li>
<li>Negative examples help define relation boundaries.</li>
</ul>
<div class="callout" data-callout="tip">
<div class="callout-title"><span class="callout-icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M8.5 14.5A2.5 2.5 0 0 0 11 12c0-1.38-.5-2-1-3-1.07-2.14-.22-4.05 2-6 .5 2.5 2 4.9 4 6.5 2 1.6 3 3.5 3 5.5a7 7 0 1 1-14 0c0-1.15.43-2.29 1-3a2.5 2.5 0 0 0 2.5 2.5Z"></path></svg></span><span class="callout-title-inner">Knowledge-Injection Dataset Design</span></div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>For each source fact, include direct QA, paraphrased QA, reverse queries where meaningful, contextual formulations, and locality controls. Avoid merely repeating one surface form.</p></div>
</div>
<h4 id="number-of-exposures-versus-number-of-unique-facts">Number of Exposures Versus Number of Unique Facts<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#number-of-exposures-versus-number-of-unique-facts">#</a></h4>
<p>Increasing training tokens can mean:</p>
<ol>
<li>Adding new facts.</li>
<li>Repeating existing facts.</li>
<li>Adding paraphrases of existing facts.</li>
<li>Adding reasoning paths connecting existing facts.</li>
</ol>
<p>These consume parameter and compute budgets differently.</p>
<p>Define:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9805em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.109em;">N</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3175em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.109em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">unique</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord vbox"><span class="thinbox"><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mord"><span class="mrel"></span></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace nobreak"></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9805em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.109em;">N</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.109em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">examples</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord vbox"><span class="thinbox"><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mord"><span class="mrel"></span></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace nobreak"></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.109em;">N</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.109em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">tokens</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>A capacity study must report all three.</p>
<p>Repetition can improve exact recall without increasing stored information. Paraphrases can improve retrieval robustness while increasing training cost. New facts increase information load directly.</p>
<h4 id="conflict-with-base-knowledge">Conflict With Base Knowledge<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#conflict-with-base-knowledge">#</a></h4>
<p>Learning a novel association and revising an existing belief are different optimization problems.</p>
<p>For a counterfactual target <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.5806em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.044em;">z</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.044em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0139em;">new</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> opposing a strong base answer <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.5806em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.044em;">z</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.044em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">old</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, the adapter must satisfy both:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.0001em;vertical-align:-0.2501em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3173em;"><span style="top:-2.357em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.143em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">ΔΘ</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2501em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.044em;">z</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.044em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight" style="margin-right:0.0139em;">new</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∣</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">↑</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>and:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.0001em;vertical-align:-0.2501em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">Θ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3173em;"><span style="top:-2.357em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.143em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mbin mtight">+</span><span class="mord mtight">ΔΘ</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2501em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.044em;">z</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.044em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">old</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∣</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">↓</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.1056em;"></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>The second requirement may consume substantial adapter capacity because the base model continually contributes the old belief through the frozen path.</p>
<p>Potential outcomes include:</p>
<ul>
<li>successful replacement;</li>
<li>context-dependent alternation;</li>
<li>answer blending;</li>
<li>overgeneralized replacement;</li>
<li>regression to the original answer under paraphrasing.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="base-model-scale-and-quality">Base-Model Scale and Quality<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#base-model-scale-and-quality">#</a></h4>
<p>A stronger base model may reduce the residual information required for structured knowledge because it already supplies:</p>
<ul>
<li>entity representations;</li>
<li>relation schemas;</li>
<li>linguistic variation;</li>
<li>reasoning primitives;</li>
<li>output formatting.</li>
</ul>
<p>However, empirical results do not support a simple monotonic law in which larger backbones always produce proportionally better LoRA memory. Improvements can be irregular because the adapter remains the principal writable component while the backbone acts as frozen infrastructure. [S4]</p>
<h2 id="capacity-generalization-and-forgetting">Capacity, Generalization, and Forgetting<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#capacity-generalization-and-forgetting">#</a></h2>
<h3 id="the-plasticitystability-trade-off">The Plasticity–Stability Trade-off<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#the-plasticitystability-trade-off">#</a></h3>
<h4 id="learning-more-usually-permits-forgetting-more">Learning More Usually Permits Forgetting More<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#learning-more-usually-permits-forgetting-more">#</a></h4>
<p>Biderman et al.'s <em>LoRA Learns Less and Forgets Less</em> reports that low-rank LoRA underperforms full fine-tuning in demanding code and mathematics adaptation, especially under continued pretraining. Full fine-tuning learned update matrices with substantially higher effective rank than standard LoRA configurations. [S5]</p>
<p>This supports the following continuum:</p>






























<table><thead><tr><th align="left">Method</th><th align="left">Plasticity</th><th align="left">Retention of base behaviour</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td align="left">Very-low-rank LoRA</td><td align="left">Low</td><td align="left">High</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Higher-rank/all-linear LoRA</td><td align="left">Medium</td><td align="left">Medium–high</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Partial full-rank tuning</td><td align="left">High</td><td align="left">Medium</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Full fine-tuning</td><td align="left">Highest</td><td align="left">Lowest without constraints</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The design principle is:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8623em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">capacity to acquire</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">↔</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8623em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">capacity to overwrite</span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>The low-rank constraint is simultaneously:</p>
<ul>
<li>a memory bottleneck;</li>
<li>a regularizer;</li>
<li>a protection against uncontrolled drift;</li>
<li>a barrier to major capability acquisition.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="new-knowledge-accuracy-can-hide-global-damage">New-Knowledge Accuracy Can Hide Global Damage<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#new-knowledge-accuracy-can-hide-global-damage">#</a></h4>
<p>Pletenev et al.'s <em>How Much Knowledge Can You Pack into a LoRA Adapter without Harming LLM?</em> finds that mixing known and new facts can improve knowledge injection, but external QA performance can still decline. Biased training data may also cause regression toward a small number of overrepresented answers. [S6]</p>
<p>A complete evaluation therefore requires:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">utility</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">new knowledge</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">retained knowledge</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">locality</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">general capability</span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Do not evaluate only the newly inserted facts.</p>
<h4 id="knowledge-update-metrics">Knowledge-Update Metrics<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#knowledge-update-metrics">#</a></h4>













































<table><thead><tr><th align="left">Metric</th><th align="left">Question answered</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td align="left"><strong>Reliability</strong></td><td align="left">Does the model answer the direct training query correctly?</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Generalization</strong></td><td align="left">Does the answer survive paraphrasing?</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Portability</strong></td><td align="left">Can the fact participate in related reasoning?</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Locality</strong></td><td align="left">Are unrelated outputs unchanged?</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Retention</strong></td><td align="left">Are previously known facts preserved?</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Specificity</strong></td><td align="left">Is the update restricted to the intended entity/relation?</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Calibration</strong></td><td align="left">Is confidence appropriate?</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Compositionality</strong></td><td align="left">Can multiple learned facts be combined?</td></tr><tr><td align="left"><strong>Reversibility</strong></td><td align="left">Can the update be removed cleanly by disabling the adapter?</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="callout" data-callout="warning">
<div class="callout-title"><span class="callout-icon" aria-hidden="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="18" height="18" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="m21.73 18-8-14a2 2 0 0 0-3.48 0l-8 14A2 2 0 0 0 4 21h16a2 2 0 0 0 1.73-3Z"></path><path d="M12 9v4"></path><path d="M12 17h.01"></path></svg></span><span class="callout-title-inner">Training Recall Is the Weakest Test</span></div>
<div class="callout-content"><p>Perfect reproduction of training prompts establishes only that the optimization problem was solved on those prompts.</p></div>
</div>
<h2 id="scaling-beyond-a-single-lora">Scaling Beyond a Single LoRA<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#scaling-beyond-a-single-lora">#</a></h2>
<h3 id="modular-parametric-memory">Modular Parametric Memory<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#modular-parametric-memory">#</a></h3>
<h4 id="multiple-small-loras-versus-one-large-lora">Multiple Small LoRAs Versus One Large LoRA<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#multiple-small-loras-versus-one-large-lora">#</a></h4>
<p>Under a fixed total parameter budget, partitioning knowledge across multiple small LoRAs can outperform one monolithic adapter if the correct module is always selected. [S7]</p>
<p>Suppose:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">total</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:3.2421em;vertical-align:-1.4138em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.8283em;"><span style="top:-1.8723em;margin-left:0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0572em;">j</span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">∑</span></span></span><span style="top:-4.3em;margin-left:0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.109em;">M</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.4138em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0572em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>A modular system stores disjoint knowledge partitions:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.0144em;">K</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:3.2421em;vertical-align:-1.4138em;"></span><span class="mop op-limits"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.8283em;"><span style="top:-1.8723em;margin-left:0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0572em;">j</span><span class="mrel mtight">=</span><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span style="top:-3.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span><span class="mop op-symbol large-op">⋃</span></span></span><span style="top:-4.3em;margin-left:0em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:3.05em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.109em;">M</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.4138em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.0144em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0144em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0572em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:2em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.0144em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0144em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∩</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9694em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.0144em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0144em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0572em;">j</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6633em;vertical-align:-0.0817em;"></span><span class="mord amsrm">∅</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Potential benefit:</p>
<ul>
<li>each adapter remains below its saturation threshold;</li>
<li>unrelated facts do not compete within one low-rank update;</li>
<li>modules can be added or removed independently;</li>
<li>updates are easier to version.</li>
</ul>
<p>Under oracle routing:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9331em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0572em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.7387em;"><span style="top:-3.113em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">Router</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>and only <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9805em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">ϕ</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0572em;">j</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.6183em;"><span style="top:-2.786em;margin-right:0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mbin mtight">∗</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is activated.</p>
<p>This converts a single-adapter capacity problem into a routing problem.</p>
<h4 id="routing-becomes-the-new-bottleneck">Routing Becomes the New Bottleneck<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#routing-becomes-the-new-bottleneck">#</a></h4>
<p>Practical embedding-based routing can perform substantially worse than oracle routing and may even underperform a single broad LoRA. [S7]</p>
<p>Error decomposition:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">correct</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">correct</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∣</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">right module</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">right module</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">correct</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∣</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">wrong module</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">wrong module</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Highly specialized modules make:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">correct</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∣</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">wrong module</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>particularly small.</p>
<p>The modular architecture therefore succeeds only if:</p>
<ul>
<li>routing recall is high;</li>
<li>knowledge partitions are semantically separable;</li>
<li>multi-hop queries can activate all relevant modules;</li>
<li>routing latency remains acceptable;</li>
<li>module identity is stable under paraphrasing.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="merging-is-not-equivalent-to-routing">Merging Is Not Equivalent to Routing<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#merging-is-not-equivalent-to-routing">#</a></h4>
<p>For adapters <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8778em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">W</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">W</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.109em;">M</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, direct merging produces:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9694em;vertical-align:-0.2861em;"></span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">W</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">merge</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2861em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span <p>This changes every query, even when only one adapter is relevant.</p>

<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span
