<p>The sum of two rank-<span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span> adapters may require rank up to <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span></span></span></span> to represent exactly.</p>
<h2 id="a-rigorous-experimental-protocol-for-measuring-lora-capacity">A Rigorous Experimental Protocol for Measuring LoRA Capacity<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#a-rigorous-experimental-protocol-for-measuring-lora-capacity">#</a></h2>
<h3 id="capacity-should-be-measured-not-assumed">Capacity Should Be Measured, Not Assumed<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#capacity-should-be-measured-not-assumed">#</a></h3>
<h4 id="research-question-definition">Research Question Definition<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#research-question-definition">#</a></h4>
<p>A defensible experiment should specify which capacity is being estimated:</p>
<ul>
<li>arbitrary key–value memorization;</li>
<li>counterfactual factual updating;</li>
<li>natural-document internalization;</li>
<li>relational generalization;</li>
<li>procedural capability acquisition;</li>
<li>domain continued pretraining.</li>
</ul>
<p>These are different dependent variables and should not be collapsed into one “knowledge capacity” score.</p>
<h4 id="controlled-dataset-construction">Controlled Dataset Construction<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#controlled-dataset-construction">#</a></h4>
<p>Use nested datasets:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9334em;vertical-align:-0.2501em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">D</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0278em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3173em;"><span style="top:-2.357em;margin-left:-0.0715em;margin-right:0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.143em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2501em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊂</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9334em;vertical-align:-0.2501em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">D</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0278em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3173em;"><span style="top:-2.357em;margin-left:-0.0715em;margin-right:0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.143em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2501em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊂</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.5782em;vertical-align:-0.0391em;"></span><span class="minner">⋯</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊂</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.9334em;vertical-align:-0.2501em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">D</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0278em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1645em;"><span style="top:-2.357em;margin-left:-0.0715em;margin-right:0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.143em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.2501em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>where <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8333em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3117em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0715em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> is the information load.</p>
<p>For each load, report:</p>
<ul>
<li>unique facts;</li>
<li>answer tokens;</li>
<li>total training tokens;</li>
<li>estimated entropy;</li>
<li>number of paraphrases;</li>
<li>number of exposures;</li>
<li>degree of conflict with base knowledge.</li>
</ul>
<p>Include:</p>
<ul>
<li>random associations to estimate raw memory;</li>
<li>natural facts to estimate compressible memory;</li>
<li>counterfactual facts to estimate revision cost;</li>
<li>unrelated controls to estimate locality.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="rank-and-placement-sweep">Rank and Placement Sweep<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#rank-and-placement-sweep">#</a></h4>
<p>At minimum, sweep:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.5782em;vertical-align:-0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">8</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">16</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">32</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">64</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">128</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">256</span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Compare:</p>
<ul>
<li>attention-only;</li>
<li>MLP-only;</li>
<li>all-linear;</li>
<li>equal total-parameter configurations;</li>
<li>uniform-rank versus non-uniform-rank allocations.</li>
</ul>
<p>The important control is to separate:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">effect of rank</span></span></span></span></span></span>
<p>from:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">effect of total parameters</span></span></span></span></span></span>
<p>and:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">effect of placement</span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<h4 id="optimization-controls">Optimization Controls<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#optimization-controls">#</a></h4>
<p>For each configuration:</p>
<ul>
<li>tune learning rate rather than reusing one value for every rank;</li>
<li>train long enough to distinguish capacity failure from undertraining;</li>
<li>report both fixed-step and convergence-matched results;</li>
<li>use several random seeds;</li>
<li>track gradient norms for <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span></span></span></span> separately;</li>
<li>inspect singular values of <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span></span>;</li>
<li>test LoRA+ or improved initialization when optimization failure is suspected.</li>
</ul>
<p>A rank may appear insufficient merely because its factorization was poorly optimized.</p>
<h4 id="evaluation-grid">Evaluation Grid<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#evaluation-grid">#</a></h4>

















































<table><thead><tr><th align="left">Axis</th><th align="left">Required test</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td align="left">Direct recall</td><td align="left">Original question</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Surface robustness</td><td align="left">Several paraphrases</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Context robustness</td><td align="left">Distractor context</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Relation reversal</td><td align="left">Ask inverse relation where valid</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Compositional use</td><td align="left">Multi-hop question</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Locality</td><td align="left">Neighbouring and unrelated facts</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Retention</td><td align="left">Base benchmark before/after</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Exactness</td><td align="left">Exact match and token accuracy</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Calibration</td><td align="left">Correct-answer probability</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Prompt sensitivity</td><td align="left">Multiple templates</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4 id="estimating-the-saturation-curve">Estimating the Saturation Curve<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#estimating-the-saturation-curve">#</a></h4>
<p>For each rank, estimate:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0715em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.1132em;">τ</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mop">max</span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">K</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mop"><span class="mord mathrm">Score</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0278em;">r</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">K</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1132em;">τ</span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Then fit, where justified:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mop">lo<span style="margin-right:0.0139em;">g</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0715em;">K</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.0715em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.1132em;">τ</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6667em;vertical-align:-0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0556em;">γ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop">lo<span style="margin-right:0.0139em;">g</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3283em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">LoRA</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">ε</span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>Interpretation:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6776em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0556em;">γ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span>: approximately linear capacity growth.</li>
<li><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6835em;vertical-align:-0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&#x3C;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7335em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0556em;">γ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&#x3C;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span>: diminishing returns.</li>
<li><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7335em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0556em;">γ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span></span></span></span>: possible reuse or compression effects.</li>
<li>Unstable <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0556em;">γ</span></span></span></span>: regime change, optimization failure, or unsuitable capacity metric.</li>
</ul>
<p>Report confidence intervals across seeds rather than only the best run.</p>
<h4 id="separating-storage-from-retrieval-failure">Separating Storage From Retrieval Failure<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#separating-storage-from-retrieval-failure">#</a></h4>
<p>When a fact is answered incorrectly, the failure may occur because:</p>
<ol>
<li>It was never encoded.</li>
<li>It was encoded but the prompt did not retrieve it.</li>
<li>The right concept was retrieved but the exact value was not.</li>
<li>A competing base-model answer dominated.</li>
<li>Autoregressive decoding failed after an early token error.</li>
<li>Another learned fact interfered.</li>
</ol>
<p>Useful probes include:</p>
<ul>
<li>teacher-forced target-token probabilities;</li>
<li>representation similarity across paraphrases;</li>
<li>logit-lens inspection;</li>
<li>activation patching;</li>
<li>nearest-neighbour analysis of hidden states;</li>
<li>singular-vector analysis of <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">Δ</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.1389em;">W</span></span></span></span>.</li>
</ul>
<p>This connects LoRA capacity research to Mechanistic Interpretability and Associative Memory.</p>
<h2 id="design-rules-for-knowledge-bearing-loras">Design Rules for Knowledge-Bearing LoRAs<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#design-rules-for-knowledge-bearing-loras">#</a></h2>
<h3 id="practical-synthesis">Practical Synthesis<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#practical-synthesis">#</a></h3>
<h4 id="capacity-provisioning-rules">Capacity Provisioning Rules<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#capacity-provisioning-rules">#</a></h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Do not choose rank from dataset row count alone</strong>: estimate unique information and conflict with the base model.</li>
<li><strong>Sweep rank on nested knowledge loads</strong>: observe the empirical saturation point.</li>
<li><strong>Prefer the smallest rank satisfying the target reliability threshold</strong>: it often maximizes efficiency and retention.</li>
<li><strong>Increase placement breadth before extreme rank</strong> when the current modules may be the bottleneck.</li>
<li><strong>Inspect effective rank</strong>: unused nominal dimensions do not provide useful capacity.</li>
<li><strong>Train on retrieval-aligned formulations</strong>: direct QA plus paraphrases usually outperforms raw exposure alone.</li>
<li><strong>Include old knowledge and locality controls</strong> when updating an existing model belief.</li>
<li><strong>Use modular LoRAs only when routing accuracy can be validated</strong>.</li>
<li><strong>Retain RAG for precise, changing, auditable information</strong>.</li>
<li><strong>Treat full fine-tuning as a capability-acquisition option</strong>, not merely a larger LoRA.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="warning-signs-of-capacity-overflow">Warning Signs of Capacity Overflow<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#warning-signs-of-capacity-overflow">#</a></h4>
<p>Possible symptoms:</p>
<ul>
<li>training loss continues falling while exact match stagnates;</li>
<li>performance falls as more facts are added;</li>
<li>frequent confusion between entities sharing the same relation;</li>
<li>regression to high-frequency answers;</li>
<li>strong dependence on the original prompt template;</li>
<li>newly learned facts disappear under distractor context;</li>
<li>larger rank improves training recall but not paraphrase recall;</li>
<li>unrelated base capabilities deteriorate;</li>
<li>effective rank reaches the nominal-rank ceiling;</li>
<li>different seeds produce sharply different results.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="decision-table">Decision Table<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#decision-table">#</a></h4>




























































<table><thead><tr><th align="left">Observed failure</th><th align="left">Likely cause</th><th align="left">Appropriate response</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td align="left">Poor train recall at all ranks</td><td align="left">Data or optimization problem</td><td align="left">Improve supervision and optimization</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Recall improves monotonically with rank</td><td align="left">Capacity-limited</td><td align="left">Increase rank or adapted modules</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Train recall high, paraphrase recall low</td><td align="left">Retrieval overfitting</td><td align="left">Add paraphrases and semantic supervision</td></tr><tr><td align="left">New facts learned, base facts damaged</td><td align="left">Excessive plasticity/interference</td><td align="left">Lower rank, mix retention data, regularize</td></tr><tr><td align="left">One large adapter saturates</td><td align="left">Internal competition</td><td align="left">Partition into modules or use RAG</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Multi-LoRA fails despite good modules</td><td align="left">Routing failure</td><td align="left">Improve router or use broader adapter</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Counterfactual fact alternates with old fact</td><td align="left">Strong frozen prior</td><td align="left">Add contrastive/revision examples</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Exact match fails after one token</td><td align="left">Decoding bottleneck</td><td align="left">Inspect token probabilities; target hard tokens</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Higher rank provides no gain</td><td align="left">Unused rank or placement bottleneck</td><td align="left">Inspect spectrum; change modules</td></tr><tr><td align="left">Need deletion, citations, or frequent updates</td><td align="left">Parametric memory mismatch</td><td align="left">Use Retrieval-Augmented Generation</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2 id="open-research-questions">Open Research Questions<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#open-research-questions">#</a></h2>
<h3 id="unresolved-theoretical-and-empirical-problems">Unresolved Theoretical and Empirical Problems<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#unresolved-theoretical-and-empirical-problems">#</a></h3>
<h4 id="a-universal-lora-capacity-law-does-not-yet-exist">A Universal LoRA Capacity Law Does Not Yet Exist<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#a-universal-lora-capacity-law-does-not-yet-exist">#</a></h4>
<p>Current power laws are empirical and regime-specific. Open questions include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Do capacity exponents remain stable above 8B models?</li>
<li>How do MoE architectures change adapter memory?</li>
<li>Does capacity scale differently for attention and MLP adapters?</li>
<li>What is the relation between effective rank and factual entropy?</li>
<li>Can capacity be predicted before training?</li>
<li>How does quantization alter writable information capacity?</li>
<li>What is the effect of optimizer precision on stored information?</li>
<li>Can relational knowledge be compressed more effectively than arbitrary facts?</li>
<li>How much apparent capacity comes from exploiting pre-existing latent features?</li>
<li>Can one distinguish knowledge encoded in <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0502em;">B</span></span></span></span>, and the frozen residual stream?</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="robust-knowledge-versus-verbatim-memory">Robust Knowledge Versus Verbatim Memory<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#robust-knowledge-versus-verbatim-memory">#</a></h4>
<p>Most controlled capacity experiments emphasize exact recall because it is easy to measure. However, doctoral-level analysis must distinguish:</p>
<span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">verbatim capacity</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord vbox"><span class="thinbox"><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mord"><span class="mrel"></span></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace nobreak"></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">semantic capacity</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mrel"><span class="mord vbox"><span class="thinbox"><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mord"><span class="mrel"></span></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace nobreak"></span><span class="mrel">=</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8623em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">reasoning capacity</span></span><span class="mord">.</span></span></span></span></span>
<p>A model that reconstructs a paragraph exactly may not answer a novel question about it. A model that cannot reconstruct it exactly may still have learned the relevant abstraction.</p>
<p>A complete theory will require separate scaling laws for:</p>
<ul>
<li>exact reconstruction;</li>
<li>semantic retrieval;</li>
<li>relational composition;</li>
<li>procedural transfer;</li>
<li>locality and forgetting.</li>
</ul>
<h4 id="adapter-capacity-as-an-alignment-question">Adapter Capacity as an Alignment Question<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#adapter-capacity-as-an-alignment-question">#</a></h4>
<p>If safety or policy behaviour is encoded through low-rank adaptation, the same capacity constraints apply:</p>
<ul>
<li>low rank may make alignment economical;</li>
<li>low rank may make alignment fragile;</li>
<li>subsequent adapters may interfere with the safety update;</li>
<li>a malicious adapter may redirect existing capabilities without learning them from scratch;</li>
<li>removing or replacing the safety adapter may expose the base behaviour.</li>
</ul>
<p>This connects LoRA memory to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Machine Unlearning;</li>
<li>Continual Learning;</li>
<li>Model Editing;</li>
<li>Catastrophic Forgetting;</li>
<li>Alignment Tax;</li>
<li>Mechanistic Interpretability;</li>
<li>Modular Neural Networks.</li>
</ul>
<p>[S1] Rank sweeps from 2–1024, controlled knowledge loads, finite saturation, and declining parameter efficiency at high rank are reported by Back et al.
[S2] The proposed power-law relationship, its 8B-model experiments, and the distinction between loss and exact recall come from Xu et al.
[S3] The 2 and approximately 3.6 bits-per-parameter results are dense-transformer estimates under different controlled definitions of knowledge and memorization, not LoRA-specific constants.
[S4] Structured QA and summary supervision, non-linear effects of base-model scale, and the limited reliability of simply switching LoRA variants are reported by Back et al.
[S5] The learning–forgetting trade-off and the substantially higher-rank updates learned by full fine-tuning are reported by Biderman et al.
[S6] The effects of mixing old and new facts, degradation on external QA, and regression toward overrepresented answers are reported by Pletenev et al.
[S7] The advantage of partitioning knowledge under oracle routing—and the degradation introduced by practical routing—is reported by Back et al.</p>
<h2 id="knowledge-capacity-review-checklist">Knowledge-Capacity Review Checklist<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" hidden href="#knowledge-capacity-review-checklist">#</a></h2>
<ul class="contains-task-list">
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" disabled> Explain why knowledge resides in the adapter–backbone interaction rather than in the LoRA alone.</li>
